# Excalidraw Data
## Text Elements
We undergo dumping, loss per cycle. ^Opyf8eeX

This characterization is equivalent to the spring model. ^TExj056N

This is from last time. ^QS0eYMaD

Xo is known as static susceptability. ^ZRBucSCA

Attained via complex conjugation by the top and bottom. ^K89UmGrX

This tells you how much you resonate with respect to the material. The imaginary part is supposed to capture the natural phase difference between the wave and the resonant frequency of the material. ^uqIGLP1C

When the incoming wave has a frequency way above the last resonance frequency, the material is practically transparent ^4pLeAeR9

You are performing a shift from the origin to w_0. This is a mathematical truth which comes from multiplying A by a complex exponential. ^ec855jsd
